   <h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">
    List of 21st-century lunar eclipses
   </h1>
   <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
    <div class="noprint" id="siteSub">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div>
    <div id="contentSub">
    </div>
    <div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
     Jump to:
     <a href="#mw-head">
      navigation
     </a>
     ,
     <a href="#p-search">
      search
     </a>
    </div>
    <div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <p>
       There will be 230
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lunar_eclipses" title="Lunar eclipses">
        lunar eclipses
       </a>
       in the 21st century (2000–2100): 87 penumbral, 58 partial and 85 total.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Eclipses are listed in sets by
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lunar_year" title="Lunar year">
        lunar years
       </a>
       , repeating every 12 months for each node. Ascending node eclipses are given a red background highlight.
      </p>
      <p>
       See also:
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_lunar_eclipses" title="List of lunar eclipses">
        List of lunar eclipses
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_20th-century_lunar_eclipses" title="List of 20th-century lunar eclipses">
        List of 20th-century lunar eclipses
       </a>
       , and
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_22nd-century_lunar_eclipses" title="List of 22nd-century lunar eclipses">
        List of 22nd-century lunar eclipses
       </a>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="List_of_lunar_eclipses_between_2000_and_2100">
        List of lunar eclipses between 2000 and 2100
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_21st-century_lunar_eclipses&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: List of lunar eclipses between 2000 and 2100">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       Eclipses from August 1998 are included to complete the first eclipse set.
      </p>
